  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_dfc3b5d6-284a-484b-9c85-1348e0659f1b'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);

<span id="freeTextContainer15539311191982272743">"You have to teach your heart and mind how to sing together... then you'll hear the sound of your soul."<br/><br/>Mia Kelly thinks she has it all figured out. She's an Ivy League graduate, a classically trained pianist, and the beloved daughter of a sensible mother and offbeat father.   <span id="freeText15539311191982272743" style="display:none">"You have to teach your heart and mind how to sing together... then you'll hear the sound of your soul."<br /><br />Mia Kelly thinks she has it all figured out. She's an Ivy League graduate, a classically trained pianist, and the beloved daughter of a sensible mother and offbeat father. Yet Mia has been stalling since graduation, torn between putting her business degree to use and exploring music, her true love.<br /><br />When her father unexpectedly dies, she decides to pick up the threads of his life while she figures out her own. Uprooting herself from Ann Arbor to New York City, Mia takes over her father's cafe, a treasured neighborhood institution that plays host to undiscovered musicians and artists. She's denied herself the thrilling and unpredictable life of a musician, but a chance encounter with Will, a sweet, gorgeous, and charming guitarist, offers her a glimpse of what could be. When Will becomes her friend and then her roommate, she does everything in her power to suppress her passions—for him, for music—but her father's legacy slowly opens her heart to the possibility of something more.<br /><br />A "heartbreaking and romantic" (Aestas Book Blog) debut, Sweet Thing explores the intensity and complexities of first love and self-discovery.</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/594604209" />

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/594604209?book_show_action=true">Apr 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mo" href="/user/show/11856352-mo">Mo</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17609127-sweet-thing">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer594604209" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3430797642849214493">Good looking guy - Check<br/>Cute girl - Check<br/>Kelly and Ryan - good Irish surnames - Check<br/>Lovable Dog - Check<br/>New York City - Check<br/>References to Music - Check<br/>No Bondage - Check<br/>No Millionaires/Billionaires/Trillionaires -CHECK, CHECK, TRIPLE CHECK!!<br/><br/>What a lovely find this was. Had been going through a bit of a slump in the book department there for a while and this one caught my eye on Goodreads. I must say we readers are very lucky with all the new talented authors emerging at the moment. This is a de</span>
  <span id="freeText3430797642849214493" style="display:none">Good looking guy - Check<br>Cute girl - Check<br>Kelly and Ryan - good Irish surnames - Check<br>Lovable Dog - Check<br>New York City - Check<br>References to Music - Check<br>No Bondage - Check<br>No Millionaires/Billionaires/Trillionaires -CHECK, CHECK, TRIPLE CHECK!!<br><br>What a lovely find this was. Had been going through a bit of a slump in the book department there for a while and this one caught my eye on Goodreads. I must say we readers are very lucky with all the new talented authors emerging at the moment. This is a debut novel by this author but you would not think it. The Prologue piqued my interest straight away and the whole book flowed along very nicely for me…. and the Epilogue was good too.<br><br>I absolutely loved all the musical references throughout the book. I am a big music fan and all these songs were great. <br><br> <br> WILL RYAN<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380303153i/687741.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> MIA KELLY<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380303153i/687742.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380303153i/687743.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380303153i/687744._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>FRIENDSHIP <br>"You have to teach your heart and mind how to sing together… the you'll hear the sound of your soul."<br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380303153i/687745._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>Awwwwww!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380303153i/687746._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br>"You've ruined me…."<br><br>"Ever has it been that love knows not its own depth until the house of separation ...."<br><br><br>I know some reviewers were not too happy with Mia and her wishy/washy couldn’t make up her mind. But, let’s remember, she had just lost her Pops, had moved to a new city, was trying to run a business, was confused about what career path to take … it is a lot to take on and then to have a certain gorgeous guy kinda fall into your lap – it would have made my head spin too.<br><br>“Remember me to one who lives there<br>For she was once a true love of mine….” – Check out the Johnny Cash/Joni Mitchell version of this...<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=W1QO0jQ0PB0">http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=W1QO0j...</a><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380303153i/687747.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Will was the hero who never gave up (well deep down he never gave up) – she needed her space, he gave it to her. It was painful, it was sad but sometimes Love Hurts…<br><br>One negative thing…. and it probably lost half a star for this. It is 4.5 but could have been 5. If I read another book where the Hero shouts “You’re Mine … Come for Me.” again, I will seriously throw my Kindle out the friggin window…. Let’s be a little bit original here. Ya Hear Me??<br><br>... and don't make the Irish guys out to be Paddys from the back arse of nowhere with their "tree tirty" instead of "three thirty" ... well it was some phrase like that - Deliver us Lord from those who think the Irish sound like Tom Cruise sounds like in "Far and Away"!<br>I am Irish and think I am qualified to make a comment like this. I was born in the "ould sod", I am not a Green Beer on Patty's Day (God I hate that phrase, Patty's Day) Oirish person... I am the Real Deal!<br><br>Other than that, it was a fairly perfect read for me.<br><br>I remember seeing Van the Man in concert many years ago and when this song was mentioned in the book, I immediately put it on to listen to. It is definitely one of my favourites of his. What a classic! <br>So crank up the stereo and let the sublime tones of Mr Morrison take you to a Higher Ground…..<br><br><i>
  <b><br>And I will stroll the merry way<br>And jump the hedges first<br>And I will drink the clear<br>Clean water for to quench my thirst<br>And I shall watch the ferry-boats<br>And they'll get high<br>On a bluer ocean<br><br>gainst tomorrow's sky<br>And I will never grow so old again<br>And I will walk and talk<br>In gardens all wet with rain<br><br>Oh sweet thing, sweet thing<br><br>My, my, my, my, my sweet thing<br>And I shall drive my chariot<br>Down your streets and cry<br>'Hey, it's me, I'm dynamite<br>And I don't know why'<br>And you shall take me strongly<br>In your arms again<br>And I will not remember<br>That I even felt the pain.<br>We shall walk and talk<br>In gardens all misty and wet with rain<br>And I will never, never, never<br>Grow so old again.<br><br>Oh sweet thing, sweet thing<br>My, my, my, my, my sweet thing<br>And I will raise my hand up<br>Into the night time sky<br>And count the stars<br>That's shining in your eye<br>Just to dig it all an' not to wonder<br>That's just fine<br>And I'll be satisfied<br>Not to read in between the lines<br>And I will walk and talk<br>In gardens all wet with rain<br>And I will never, ever, ever, ever<br>Grow so old again.<br>Oh sweet thing, sweet thing<br>Sugar-baby with your champagne eyes<br>And your saint-like smile....<br></b>
</i><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=2QzDWIOUnM0">http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=2QzDWI...</a><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380303153i/687748.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Share your music<br>Share your words <br>Share your love <br>Your passion<br>You fears<br>Your hopes<br>And your Dreams <br>Share your precious heart<br>Share your wild mind <br>Share your special soul with me <br>And I promise to <br>Give you all of mine<br> <br><br>Yes, it was a roller-coaster ride to find ....…. cosmic, soul-shattering, air in your lungs kind of love.<br><br><span>[image error]</span><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380909230i/3178529.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>With my eyes wide open<br>I see the secrets in the rain<br>I see the loss, see the pain<br>I see you've lost your way again<br>No lines drawn<br>No boundaries made<br>Dance with me tonight, pretty baby<br>And let me pray<br>Don't let me hear you cry<br>Save your dream<br>Feed your fear<br>I'll hold you forever here<br>I need the rain to cleanse my soul<br>It tortures me, it makes me whole<br>I need the rain, I need it all<br>No lines drawn<br>No boundaries made<br>Just stay with me tonight, pretty baby<br>And let me pray….<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="3430797642849214493" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer5193287128322688302">I know I am six years late to this particular party, but my reading advisor, Robin Hill, recently supplied me with a fantastic list of books she loved and figured I would as well. This gem was on that list, and once again, her instincts were spot on.<br/><br/>With blinders fully in place, I opened to the prologue and it wasn’t long before I was in angst heaven!<br/><br/>I must forewarn you about the main characters, Will and Mia. Will oozes sex appeal and is adorable X 10. Mia ... well, she will most likely get on </span>
  <span id="freeText5193287128322688302" style="display:none">I know I am six years late to this particular party, but my reading advisor, Robin Hill, recently supplied me with a fantastic list of books she loved and figured I would as well. This gem was on that list, and once again, her instincts were spot on.<br /><br />With blinders fully in place, I opened to the prologue and it wasn’t long before I was in angst heaven!<br /><br />I must forewarn you about the main characters, Will and Mia. Will oozes sex appeal and is adorable X 10. Mia ... well, she will most likely get on your nerves a time or two. Ah geez, who am I kidding, at least a half dozen times ;)<br /><br />Although Will and Mia’s chemistry was palpable, this my friends, is how you write an engaging slow burn romance. I loved how playing music together was their aphrodisiac.<br /><br />A total page turner, and I savored every word.</span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_606109763" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/606109763" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/606109763?book_show_action=true">May 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17609127-sweet-thing">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer606109763" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16250819285586695593"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380303153i/687736._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380303153i/687737._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> I have a new book boyfriend and his name is Will Ryan. I’m in love. Oh, and did I mention he was a bit of a rockstar?? ;)<br/><br/>Sweet Thing was a sweet, heartbreaking and romantic story that kept me up reading all night! </b> 4.5 stars.<br/><br/>This was one of those books that shifted my entire TBR. I had other plans but suddenly I felt compelled to read it.<br/><br/>I’ll admit though I was hesitant to start it at first because I’d heard about some people being frustrated with the heroine, but then I realized that a lot of </span>
  <span id="freeText16250819285586695593" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380303153i/687736._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380303153i/687737._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> I have a new book boyfriend and his name is Will Ryan. I’m in love. Oh, and did I mention he was a bit of a rockstar?? ;)<br><br>Sweet Thing was a sweet, heartbreaking and romantic story that kept me up reading all night! </b> 4.5 stars.<br><br>This was one of those books that shifted my entire TBR. I had other plans but suddenly I felt compelled to read it.<br><br>I’ll admit though I was hesitant to start it at first because I’d heard about some people being frustrated with the heroine, but then I realized that a lot of my favorite books (Thoughtless and Beautiful Disaster for example) had frustrating heroines at times too and I still loved them so I didn’t want that to hold me back from giving this a shot.<br><br><blockquote> <i>“…sometimes we figure things out and then life changes and we have to figure it all out again.” </i>
</blockquote>  <br>Hit hard by the death of her father, Mia decides to move to NYC for a while to sort through his things and take over the cafe he ran. On her way, a chance meeting in an airport crosses her paths with a gorgeous musician, Will. Something about them just clicks and they spend the entire flight talking about their shared love of music.<br><br>Turns out she has an apartment for rent and he’s looking for a new place to stay and shortly afterwards they become roommates. Mia insists on keeping things strictly platonic between them – ignoring the pull she feels towards him. She has her life planned out ahead of her – she wants a life partner who can give her stability. Her father was a musician and her parents split when she was young giving her the fear that a relationship with Will, who is so much like her father in spirit, will just end up breaking her heart and so she strongly resists the temptation.<br><br><blockquote> <i> <b> “And so it began, my secret and suppressed obsession with the sensitive, tortured, artist soul. An obsession I was still fighting tooth and nail and one I wouldn’t admit to anyone, namely myself.” </b></i>
</blockquote>  <br>This book is about her journey of realizing the important things with life. It’s heart breaking at times, frustrating and painful, but there are also sweet, beautiful moments that shine though.<br><br>Music plays a huge part in this book. Will is a musician on the brink of fame, Mia plays nearly every instruments, and her father lived and breathed music as well. The story is full of musical references that tie everything together.<br><br>Will is now on my list of favorite rockstar boyfriends. With his crooked smile, tattoos and an adorable fear of flying, he was hard not to fall for. I don’t think he could have been more adorable if he tried. He was just so sweet, loving, and so endlessly PATIENT not to mention gorgeous and talented as well. Oh, and he cuddled Mia’s dog at night when it was sick. I dare you to read that scene and not have your heart just melt into a puddle of goo. <br><br>As frustrating as Mia could be at times, I still really liked her character – especially her love of compound swear words, lol.<br><br><blockquote> <i> “There are at least five swear words I like better than fuck. My favorites are compound words like apeshit, craphat or batshit, but above all, my numero uno, all-time favorite swear word is assclown, without a doubt. Asshat runs a close second. I must say, very few things give me greater pleasure than calling someone an assclown when they really fit the bill. I love it more than puppies and baby seals.” </i>
</blockquote> <br>I guess no one is perfect and she wasn’t trying to be mean or heartless about pushing him away, she was just scared. Scared of where things could go, scared of ending up with a broken heart. And despite the fact that her heart was always pointing her towards Will, she fought long and hard to follow her head instead.<br><br><blockquote> <i> <b> “My real fear was that I would fall in love with Will or that I already had and then he would just leave me alone, broken and pathetic.” </b></i>
</blockquote>  <br><br>But it just made my heart break each time she pushed him away. I could see how badly it was hurting him and I just wanted to shake her!! I mean, tell me this isn’t heartbreaking:<br><br><blockquote> <i> <b> “He looked so pathetic standing there, rejected. He corrected himself a couple of times when his body made involuntary movements to reach out and touch me. He was fighting the urge just to simply take my hand or kiss my cheek. I didn’t know why I was being so harsh… The charade and the constant touching created so much confusion. I couldn’t tell anymore what we were to each other.” </b></i>
</blockquote>  <br>The middle of the book was painful for me, but not in a way that made me dislike the book, just in a way that hurt. It had what I’d call quiet angst. It didn’t make me want to rip my hair out or throw my kindle, but I still just wanted to shake sense into Mia and scream in her face that what she was looking for was standing right in front of her. Will was just so perfect and clearly so desperately in love with her ♥<br><br><blockquote> <i> <b> ”Just let me kiss your mouth,” he whispered, his eyes pleading.“ </b></i>
</blockquote>  <br>How do you say no to that??? He just kept giving and giving and it hurt to watch his heart being broken no matter how well he tried to hide it and say he was okay just being friends. But his patience with her was a huge part of why I loved him so much. It was like a part of him understood that she needed to go through her process and he was willing to wait.<br><br><blockquote> <b> <i> “Don’t be silly, Will is no dummy.” She paused for a long second. “He’s in love with you.”<br><br>“How do you know?”<br><br>“I can tell and anyways, he told me. I believe his exact words were cosmic, soul-shattering, air in your lungs kind of love.” </i></b>
</blockquote>  <br>But I tried to see things from her perspective, and understand what she was afraid of. See, technically she had a valid fear in a certain respect…. But what it came down to was her needing to decide what was worth the risk and whether she could bring herself to take that leap of faith and put her heart out on the line in exchange for a beautiful relationship.<br><br>Now, this isn’t a love triangle story technically, but there are other relationships that happen on the side. I guess you could say they’re mistake ones. But you would tell always that they were wrong and they never lasted. It was always Will and Mia at the heart of it all, but it just took Mia a long time to give in to that fact.<br><br>Despite romance playing a huge, central role in this book, it’s also just as much a journey of Mia’s self discovery, of piecing together her past, and in doing so finding what was holding her back from Will in the first place.<br><br>And in case you’re wondering about the title of the book: “sweet thing”. It’s what Will calls her, right from the start of the book. C’mon, tell me that’s not just fucking adorable??? *melt*<br><br>I’ve been asked if it’s a rockstar book and… hmmmm, yes and no. I guess you could call it one. Will does become a bit of a rockstar and there are all the associated issues that go with being with someone on the brink of fame. As I said, music plays a huge part in this story, as does him becoming a little bit famous, but that isn’t the central theme of the story, it’s more just a part of it.<br><br>The story is very well written. The writing is smooth and captivating and keeps you totally immersed in the story. I read it in one sitting and didn’t want to put it down.<br><br>I loved Will and Mia and really enjoyed their story. I wish they (well, Mia) hadn’t made so many choices that kept them apart but that’s kind of the way life is, right? It’s imperfect and the journey isn’t always smooth but thankfully their story had a beautiful, happy ending (epilogue and all) that left me smiling.<br><br><blockquote> <i> <b> “He buried his face in my neck and pulled me into a hug. I threw my arms around him and whispered, “Never let me go.”<br><br>He tightened his grip as his mouth moved to my ear. <br><br>“Never.” </b></i>
</blockquote>  <br>Sweet Thing was a fabulous debut novel and I’ll be watching out for more from Renee Carlino!<br><br>4 – 4.5 stars. I want to give it 4.5 but some of Mia’s decisions keep pushing it back to 4, and then Will’s sweetness strongly keeps bumping it right back up to 4.5… so I guess it’ll rest somewhere in between, but closer to 4.5 ;)<br><br>CASTING (See above and below)<br><br>I couldn't decide which pic I liked more for Will so I left them both:<br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380303153i/687738._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>or maybe this? <br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380303153i/687739._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1363208437l/17609127.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="16250819285586695593" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_593727868" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/593727868" />
    <a title="Jamie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11971939-jamie"><img alt="Jamie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1450934094p2/11971939.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/593727868?book_show_action=true">Apr 18, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jamie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jamie" href="/user/show/11971939-jamie">Jamie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17609127-sweet-thing">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Jamie by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/11143936-amber-rose">Amber Rose</a>
  </div>


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer593727868" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8805212732541130448"><i>
  <b> LOVED THIS STORY!!!</b>
</i><br/><br/><br/><i>
  <b> WILL ♥♥♥♥♥... </b>
</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380303153i/687741.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>I loved this book.. every single angsty heart clenching moment--and this book was full of them..!!<br/><br/>Mia has recently moved to New York City from her home in Michigan. Her dad recently died and she's come to take over his cafe and live in his apartment until she figures out what exactly she wants to do in her life. She's young and recently through with college. This story is told from her POV. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380909230i/3178542.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>On the flight to NYC she meets Will.. he's seated next to her a</span>
  <span id="freeText8805212732541130448" style="display:none"><i>
  <b> LOVED THIS STORY!!!</b>
</i><br><br><br><i>
  <b> WILL ♥♥♥♥♥... </b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380303153i/687741.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I loved this book.. every single angsty heart clenching moment--and this book was full of them..!!<br><br>Mia has recently moved to New York City from her home in Michigan. Her dad recently died and she's come to take over his cafe and live in his apartment until she figures out what exactly she wants to do in her life. She's young and recently through with college. This story is told from her POV. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380909230i/3178542.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>On the flight to NYC she meets Will.. he's seated next to her and freaking out about flying. Initially she tries to ignore him but that doesn't last long. It's hard to ignore Will... He's sexy as hell and a charmer. He's totally different from what she's normally attracted to. He's got some tattoos and is a little scruffy around the edges.. he's also a musician and plays the guitar.. They laugh and cut up on the plane and she feels like she's made a friend. I won't go into all the details of how it happens but he ends up renting out one of the rooms in her apartment with her STRICT rule that they will only be friends. <br><br>The attraction was immediate once he was in the the apartment but she was determined that Will was not they type of guy she wanted and she wasnt going to make things complicated by hooking up with him since he lived with her. <br><br>Will... *sigh*... he was so f'king dreamy.. I loved that man.. he was so sweet and caring and he was so totally into Mia. He wanted her so bad but she kept up this wall in between them that she wouldnt step over. She started dating the type of man she "thought" she should be with and he was nothing like Will..<br><br><i>
  <b> HERE COMES THE HEART WRENCHING ANGST!!!</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417323ra/825251.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>This book almost killed me for a large part-- Will wanted Mia//Mia wanted Will.. but Mia did not WANT to want Will.... so she kept hurting Will over with her actions. In turn, Will would would try to get on with his life knowing he couldnt have her and this in turn would hurt Mia. This went on for a while. Are you familiar with Abby from Beautiful disaster? Well multiply how much she pissed you off by 10 and you'll have Mia. I wanted to smack this girl around so bad. Just thinking of the pain she caused Will still makes my heart constrict days later after I've finished this book. <br><br>But still---even though all the incredibly painful angst..it was such a good story. You get to see Mia grow and become the person she was meant to be.. and this is due in large part to Will. You also see Will become more than he was before Mia. It was such a long twisty road for them to get to where they needed to be. And yes.. there was a sweet beautiful HEA that left me with a huge smile and tears in my eyes at the end. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/396381.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I'm in awe that this was Renee Carlino's first book.. it was just so so good.. I did not skim a single part of this book-- I couldnt turn the pages fast enough!! And I must thank Amber (Amber Reading Room) for the book recommendation. I was all set to read another book when I got her rec and the blurb made me want to read it right away and I finished it in under a day. I am really looking forward to what Renee puts out there next. <br><br>I would recommend this book to anyone that loves the sexy sweet musician with the heart of gold and also loves to have your heart torn apart but the put back together in the best way.. <br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="8805212732541130448" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_596534856" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/596534856" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/596534856?book_show_action=true">Apr 21, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17609127-sweet-thing">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer596534856" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer759979471508967162"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/10218599-0316-4a7e-beea-cec7e7dd3e24_zps2a3ed550.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418533i/828773.jpg' alt=' photo 10218599-0316-4a7e-beea-cec7e7dd3e24_zps2a3ed550.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><i>Sweet Thing</i> was a really sweet read. It was a beautiful and touching story of two people, Mia and Will, who meet coincidentally and both of their lives change forever. <br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/1f328ae5-7750-45cd-9b0d-ff8f8ee4d435_zps2ae22d8b.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418533i/828774._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 1f328ae5-7750-45cd-9b0d-ff8f8ee4d435_zps2ae22d8b.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Mia Kelly is moving from her home in Ann Arbor to NYC. Her father has recently passed away, and she is going to the city to take over his cafe. She is responsible, has a business degree, but her real passion is music. Not only is she grieving her father, but she is trying to figure out what she wants to do with he</span>
  <span id="freeText759979471508967162" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/10218599-0316-4a7e-beea-cec7e7dd3e24_zps2a3ed550.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418533i/828773.jpg" alt=" photo 10218599-0316-4a7e-beea-cec7e7dd3e24_zps2a3ed550.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>Sweet Thing</i> was a really sweet read. It was a beautiful and touching story of two people, Mia and Will, who meet coincidentally and both of their lives change forever. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/1f328ae5-7750-45cd-9b0d-ff8f8ee4d435_zps2ae22d8b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418533i/828774._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 1f328ae5-7750-45cd-9b0d-ff8f8ee4d435_zps2ae22d8b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Mia Kelly is moving from her home in Ann Arbor to NYC. Her father has recently passed away, and she is going to the city to take over his cafe. She is responsible, has a business degree, but her real passion is music. Not only is she grieving her father, but she is trying to figure out what she wants to do with her life. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/7cb7e603-7bf3-44bb-874d-8588fa37aa57_zps0d39b847.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418533i/828775.jpg" alt=" photo 7cb7e603-7bf3-44bb-874d-8588fa37aa57_zps0d39b847.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Will Ryan knows exactly what he wants to do with his life. Music. Music is his life. He loves to play, sing, write, and he is very talented. He and Mia happen to be on the same flight on their way to NYC. They connect on the flight, just click. She runs into him again and offers to rent a room out to him in her apartment. They become best friends. <br><b>
  <blockquote>Sometimes it takes the love of others to show us who we really are. </blockquote>
</b><br>Okay everyone- I have a new book boyfriend, and his name is <b>Will Ryan</b>. Yes. I loved Will. How could you not? Musician with tattoos, the sweetest guy ever, charismatic, personable, and funny. He is exuberant and has such a passion for music and life. I just adored him. Will gets Mia to see life in a whole new way. Open her eyes to whats right in front of her. See what real possibilities exist for her. A chance to follow her dreams, do what she loves and what makes her happy. Not what she is ‘supposed’ to do. He is able to reach her and heal her in a way no one else has. Mia is still hesitant. She still can’t get out of her own head that she needs to be with the guy who can provide for her, with real ambitions. I really loved Mia’s character, but for a while, she infuriated me. I was frustrated with her for a large part of the book, but I understood some of it... <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I’m surprised that you can’t see what everyone else can.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>Mia means so much to Will. He wants her as more than a friend, but he will take her anyway he can get her. <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/f3903cc2-22f5-4c6e-8bb6-04b0be4086f3_zps873dd391.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418533i/828776.jpg" alt=" photo f3903cc2-22f5-4c6e-8bb6-04b0be4086f3_zps873dd391.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>My favorite parts of this story were when the two of them were just together, happy, making music, enjoying each other. I loved the build between the two of them.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/63a07ca8-4f99-4d62-8e7c-d2201f79990c_zps769655ca.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418533i/828777.jpg" alt=" photo 63a07ca8-4f99-4d62-8e7c-d2201f79990c_zps769655ca.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>My heart broke for Will over and over again. Mia just pushes and pushes him away. Mia has gone through so much, she just couldn’t get it together. For a while, she does. Will and Mia together... perfection.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/b78dfdb1-d2dc-4329-b892-c979cbc55648_zps0aeac8c2.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418533i/828778.jpg" alt=" photo b78dfdb1-d2dc-4329-b892-c979cbc55648_zps0aeac8c2.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Mia finally see’s past herself and gives Will and herself a chance to be happy together. And they are. For a little while. Will is getting bigger and bigger in the industry. Labels are wanting to sign him, but Will is the type of guy that has to be true to himself and his music. He won’t compromise or change who he is for anyone. It’s an admirable quality, but Mia misconstrues everything and really screws things up between them. Big time. She hurts Will in a pretty unforgivable way.<br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“The pain of losing someone is always worse when you know you could have prevented it.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b> My heart not only broke for Will during this part of the story, but for Mia as well. I was an emotional mess. I wanted this couple to pull through more than anything. Mia hurt Will in a big way. She feels terrible. She’s not really living anymore, her friends are concerned. A lot of time passes before she can finally get herself together. And she is willing to do anything to make it right between them.<br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/42974fcd-649b-44bf-9b4d-e2252bdc10fe_zps0bf3d358.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418533i/828779.jpg" alt=" photo 42974fcd-649b-44bf-9b4d-e2252bdc10fe_zps0bf3d358.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>‘Never let me go.’<br>‘Never’<br>‘Where have you been?’<br>‘Waiting for you.’</i><br><br><br>Do you ever have a book that sits on your e-reader and sits on your e-reader. You are constantly meaning to get around to it, but weeks go by and you still haven’t read it? This is constantly happening to me. Too many books, not enough time I guess. But this is one of those books that makes me want to kick my own ass for waiting so long to read it. Don’t make the same mistake I made, get to this one asap! I can’t believe this is a debut novel. It is well written and compelling. The story moved me, the music moved me. I fell in love with these characters. Not only were Mia and Will amazing, but the supporting characters were as well. A story I won’t be forgetting anytime soon! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/4d918ed3-e38e-4ceb-bd9b-2171a3a0d6e7_zps9659e83e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418533i/828780.jpg" alt=" photo 4d918ed3-e38e-4ceb-bd9b-2171a3a0d6e7_zps9659e83e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>‘Love life and life will love you back.’</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><i>ARC kindly provided by author, Renee Carlino, via Netgalley in exchange for an honest review.</i></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17609127-sweet-thing">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer610252857" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12765864839110696796">4.5 SWEET STARS.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420824i/835278._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='500' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Cutest, most endearing and frustrating book I've read this year. I'm pretty convinced that from the first page I knew I would fall a little in love with this book and here's the reason why ...<br/><br/>WILBUR RYAN.<br/><br/>Now for reviewing's sake heres some of my book thoughts ...<br/><br/>The characters ...<br/>Well we have already established that I'm a firm fan of one of the leading characters, so I'll tell you a bit more about them. Mia is incredibly sweet, determined, talented and a whole lot of lost. Her c</span>
  <span id="freeText12765864839110696796" style="display:none">4.5 SWEET STARS.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420824i/835278._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Cutest, most endearing and frustrating book I've read this year. I'm pretty convinced that from the first page I knew I would fall a little in love with this book and here's the reason why ...<br><br>WILBUR RYAN.<br><br>Now for reviewing's sake heres some of my book thoughts ...<br><br>The characters ...<br>Well we have already established that I'm a firm fan of one of the leading characters, so I'll tell you a bit more about them. Mia is incredibly sweet, determined, talented and a whole lot of lost. Her character teetered on a level of annoying most of the way through the book, but I understood the authors point and found her inner ramblings true to character. Will is a typical charmer, he always has a smile or a wink to give out and I fell for his humorous and cheeky behaviour. I have no doubt that his gregarious ways will grab any readers attention. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420824i/835279._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420824i/835280._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What's the story ...<br>Mia is recovering from her pops death she moves to New York to take over his business and start to make sense of her mid twenties existence without her father. On her plane journey Over the new York she meets aspiring artist and all round charming and gorgeous Will they hit it off immediately ~ the respective love of music tying them together ... Another chance meeting seals the deal with fate and Will moves in as Mia's housemate. Mia has already made the decision that her and will are destined to be 'just' friends, but what they don't realise is that love is round the corner ready to make its appearance, and a friendship can often be sweetest thing.<br><br>What I loved ..<br>Great chapter titles, Irresistible, adorable and charming characters. The best first encounter I've read about, a frustrating push and pull take of a friends to something more story. The beautiful story telling from the author and fabulous music references. There is no doubt I'll be reading more from this author, I ate this novel up, it has a like-ability factor that I'm convinced with sell itself to most.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420824i/835281._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Why not five ...<br>One word - Mia, as much as I understood what the author was trying to achieve this character frustrated me no end, and at times I did not like how she treated will or their friendship. With that being said I don't want to focus on the negative as I really was wrapped up in this musically loved up soirée.<br><br>Final thoughts ...<br>This story is a breath of fresh, romance air, I challenge anyone to not find something likeable about this story. Full of sweet and cute and a personable feel to it I applaud the author for bringing a love story alive. <br><br>❤❤"Love life, and life will love you back."<br><br>❤❤"You have to teach your heart and mind how to sing together ... Then you'll hear the sound of your soul."<br><br>❤❤“The pain of losing someone is always worse when you know you could have prevented it.” <br><br>❤❤“Yes, committing yourself to someone requires a leap of faith—that’s why it’s so hard for some.” <br><br>4.5 WILBUR RYAN STARS<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420824i/835282._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="12765864839110696796" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_593158153" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/593158153" />
    <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister"><img alt="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1486056026p2/4971692.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/593158153?book_show_action=true">Apr 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister">Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17609127-sweet-thing">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=music">music</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer593158153" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6579335366217714126"><b>
  <i>Sometimes it takes the love of others to show us who we really are...</i>
</b><br/><br/><i>Sweet Thing</i> was a truly refreshing read! What I loved most about this book was its incredible depth. If you were to judge this story by its pretty cover and adorable title, you might expect a sweet and tender love story--but what you're given is substantially more.<br/><br/>This story provides such powerful <b>wisdom</b>—offered in bundles and in subtle whispers. It kicks off with one of the most intriguing and well thought out prologues I'</span>
  <span id="freeText6579335366217714126" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>Sometimes it takes the love of others to show us who we really are...</i>
</b><br><br><i>Sweet Thing</i> was a truly refreshing read! What I loved most about this book was its incredible depth. If you were to judge this story by its pretty cover and adorable title, you might expect a sweet and tender love story--but what you're given is substantially more.<br><br>This story provides such powerful <b>wisdom</b>—offered in bundles and in subtle whispers. It kicks off with one of the most intriguing and well thought out prologues I've read in a while--really setting the stage for the insightful tone generously present throughout. I love how this unique introduction creatively ties into the heart of the story.<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=apfvxx" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="259" width="425" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418039i/827453.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Mia Kelly</b> thinks with her head, and doesn't let her heart lead her through life. She is a talented musician, but stubbornly pushes her passions aside as she focuses on obtaining a sensible business degree. However, all of her perfectly planned out decisions come to a crashing halt when she meets the sexy, slightly neurotic, and adorably passionate musician, Will. <br><br><b>Will Ryan</b> is full of life and abundantly lives up to his name; his strong willed character was an inspiration and I loved him the second he whipped out his rosary beads! Will is guided through life by passion, and refuses to sell-out or conform to what is expected of him. Although he and Mia had music in common, Will possessed an inner-strength that Mia lacked by remaining true to himself always. <br><br>The <b>romance</b> in this story was slow building--which I always find extremely refreshing. I adored the genuine feel of the 'friendship first' process and its gradual progression truly allowed the love to ignite when finally recognized. <br><br><b>Music</b> and art saturated these pages—the love for it; the knowledge of it; and its poetic display were all equally and beautifully portrayed. I've never wanted to jump inside the pages of a book so badly before, just so I could listen to the music being played. It was described with such an intricate grace that I almost felt like I <i>could</i> hear it...but I was thankfully able to <b>
  <i>feel</i>
</b> every little bit of it. <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2qjvhhz" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418039i/827454.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br> The writing was eloquent, insightful, and truly allowed the characters to become relatable.This touching story became such a lovely example of breaking down those protective walls that guard us, and having the <b>faith</b> to go forward. After all, the barricades we build around our hearts may protect us for a while, but never allow us to <i>truly</i> thrive in their presence. <br><br><b>
  <i>You have to teach your heart and mind how to sing together...then you'll hear the sound of your soul.</i>
</b><br><br><i>*This was a birthday buddy read with my girls! Thanks for joining me, ladies, even though I severely trailed the read!!*</i><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2mh7uop" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="50" width="50" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380347313i/701667.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>
  <u>Book Stats:</u>
</b><br><b>▪	 Genre/Category:</b> Romance/New Adult<br><b>▪	 Steam Caliber:</b> Moderate/Steamy<br><b>▪ Romance:</b> Gradual/Friendship-first. Sexual tension. Solid connection.<br><b>▪	 Characters:</b> Adorable, sexy, passionate, musician hero. Guarded, strong but sweet heroine. <br><b>▪	 Plot:</b> Uniquely executed. Centered on finding that balance between listening to your mind, and having the faith to follow your heart. Awesome prologue!<br><b>▪ Writing:</b> Developed and lyrical; engaging. <br><b>▪ POV:</b> 1st Person: Heroine<br><b>▪	 Cliffhanger:</b> None/Standalone<br><br><a href="http://prettywordsbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412050368i/11316768.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/Pretty-Words-Book-Blog/860331017317983" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height='“40"' width="150" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413062455i/11461733._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="6579335366217714126" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/593789759?book_show_action=true">Apr 18, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17609127-sweet-thing">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=arc-or-netgalley">arc-or-netgalley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=2013-release">2013-release</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=standalone">standalone</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=swoonworthy-male-lead">swoonworthy-male-lead</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer593789759" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8955158261081506491"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You have to teach your heart and mind how to sing together...then you'll hear the sound of your soul."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418130i/827722.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>4 STARS for this <b>SWEET, HEARTWARMING, MEANINGFUL, TOUCHING STORY</b> about love, loss, friendship, music and so much more. It's a story about two people trying to come to terms with their past and trying to find a way to realize their hopes and dreams together in the city of New York. <br/><br/><b>Mia --</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418130i/827723.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Will --</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418130i/827724._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>After reading this story's thoughtful, original and intriguing prologue, I knew I was in f</span>
  <span id="freeText8955158261081506491" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You have to teach your heart and mind how to sing together...then you'll hear the sound of your soul."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418130i/827722.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>4 STARS for this <b>SWEET, HEARTWARMING, MEANINGFUL, TOUCHING STORY</b> about love, loss, friendship, music and so much more. It's a story about two people trying to come to terms with their past and trying to find a way to realize their hopes and dreams together in the city of New York. <br><br><b>Mia --</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418130i/827723.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Will --</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418130i/827724._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>After reading this story's thoughtful, original and intriguing prologue, I knew I was in for an unforgettable read and that's exactly what this book turned out to be. From the moment I started reading it, I could not put it down and I ended up devouring it in one day.<br><br>Mia and Will meet each other on a plane to New York City. Will has been living there for quite some time, while Mia is heading there to take over her recently deceased father's cafe. After they land, Will promises to stop by at the cafe some time so they can chat over a cup of coffee, and he keeps true to his promise. When they meet each other again, Mia mentions that she's looking for a room mate to share her father's old apartment with and before she realizes it, Will, who was looking for a new place to live himself, has taken her up on the offer of becoming her new room mate.<br><br><b>
  <i>"The idea that I just invited a relative stranger, who owns nothing, to live in my apartment gave me a stomachache, but the weird thing was that I felt like I had known him forever."</i>
</b><br><br>Although they haven't know each other for a long time, they both feel comfortable living together. They become room mates and best friends, and although it takes them a long time to realize it, their friendship slowly but surely evolves into something much more... <br><br><u>
  <b>Mia </b>
</u><br><br>At first I really liked Mia; she seemed to be an open-minded, talented, adventurous young girl and a character I could easily relate to. But as the story progressed, the way she acted started to irritate me more and more and I had to ask myself:<p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/307090.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Seriously, the way she <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[kept pushing Will away while he was being nothing but sweet and kind to her, and the way she treated him like a loser for not selling out his soul in order to gain a promising record deal and earn a lot of money. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. Yep, that made me really *really* dislike her, a lot. I even think Mia might be one of the most frustrating female characters I've ever come across. Still, she had some good qualities too and she was a remarkable musician. I do understand why it was so hard for her to let people in and let herself be vulnerable <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[knowing that Will was a rock artist and would probably be away on tour a lot of times <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, but still, it wasn't easy to read the way she treated Will and some of her other close friends sometimes. Luckily, towards the ending, she really changed her attitude and I ended up understanding her reasonings much better.<br><br><b><u>Will </u></b><br><br><b><i>"Hey, little firecracker, you like taunting me, don't you?"</i></b><br><br>From the moment, Will and Mia meet on the plane, there's an easy banter between the two of them. They often tease each other and make each other laugh, but at the same time they can also be open to each other about their past. Because their each other's best friends for a long time before evolving into something more they really get to know each other's deepest secrets and they really just want the other person to be happy. It was refreshing to read a story that wasn't about insta-love/lust but about a slow-building kind of love, based on a solid friendship.<br><br><b><i>"You're beautiful and amazing and you have a special soul, Mia. You deserve the best."</i></b><br><br>*SWOON*<br><br></p><p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/519760.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I really loved Will. He was sweet, caring and always trying to make Mia happy. He was always there to support her and stand by her no matter what. It was obvious he had deeper feelings for Mia but he never pushed her into wanting something more. Instead he gave her all the time she needed to realize how she really felt about him. Will was a very talented musician on the verge of major breakthrough and I loved how he still tried to makes as much time for Mia and how he showed her his true feelings through his song lyrics.<br><br></p><p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380418130ra/827725.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I also loved the many music references throughout the story; especially the ones of the song called Sweet Thing by Van Morrison because "sweet thing" was the nickname Will often gave to Mia. <br><br><i>"And you shall take me strongly in your arms again<br>And I will not remember that I even felt the pain<br>And we shall walk and talk in gardens all misty and wet with rain<br>And I will never, never, never grow so old again<br>Oh sweet thing, sweet thing oh, my, my, my, my, sweet thing."<br><b>~ Van Morrison's "Sweet Thing"</b></i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418130i/827726._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br></p><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"It's a fool who thinks love will set you free. Love equals a morbid and relentless fear of losing the other person. To love is brave and Will was the bravest person I knew."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Overall, I really enjoyed reading this story and would highly recommend it to anyone who's looking for a thought provoking romance story with a little bit of angst!<br><br>I think the author <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/search/search?q=Renee%20Carnilo" title="Renee Carnilo" rel="nofollow noopener">Renee Carnilo</a> did an outstanding job at writing this debut novel and I'm already looking forward to reading much more of her work!<br><br><br><b>
  <i>**ARC courtesy of the author via Netgalley in exchange for an honest review**</i>
</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1234103057?book_show_action=true">Mar 22, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jasmine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jasmine" href="/user/show/31339793-jasmine">Jasmine</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1234103057" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16025234470622252092"><b>4 STARS! ★★★★</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427821152i/14324225.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>
  <b>“You have to teach your heart and mind how to sing together... then you'll hear the sound of your soul.”</b>
</i><br/><br/>Holy motha of emotions. I never thought I'd live to see a day where a book could have pushed all my buttons like <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13517535.Thoughtless__Thoughtless___1_' title='Thoughtless (Thoughtless, #1) by S.C. Stephens' rel='nofollow noopener'>Thoughtless</a> did and to go through a heroine as frustrating as Kiera all over again (minus the cheating and love triangle, thankfully). All I wanted to do is set my Kindle on fire repeatedly or throw it against the wall in hopes that it'll somehow be enough to knock </span>
  <span id="freeText16025234470622252092" style="display:none"><b>4 STARS! ★★★★</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427821152i/14324225.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>“You have to teach your heart and mind how to sing together... then you'll hear the sound of your soul.”</b>
</i><br><br>Holy motha of emotions. I never thought I'd live to see a day where a book could have pushed all my buttons like <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13517535.Thoughtless__Thoughtless___1_" title="Thoughtless (Thoughtless, #1) by S.C. Stephens" rel="nofollow noopener">Thoughtless</a> did and to go through a heroine as frustrating as Kiera all over again (minus the cheating and love triangle, thankfully). All I wanted to do is set my Kindle on fire repeatedly or throw it against the wall in hopes that it'll somehow be enough to knock some sense into the heroine, Mia. <br><br>I swooned, I yelled, I cried and I raged a helluva lot that it left me so worn out by the end of the book. <b>But did I love this book?</b> Without a doubt, YES. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427478435i/14274945.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Honestly, this book left me in a mess. Where do I even begin? The prologue itself was already so thought-provoking and original, the writing was absolutely poignant and beautiful that I just <i>knew</i> that this read is gonna be different. Throw in an adorably chance encounter between both MCs on an airplane, little did I know I was going to be swept away by a hurricane of a story that is <u>Sweet Thing</u>.<br><br>This is a story of <b>Mia Kelly</b> who moves in to New York after her dad passed away and left behind his cafe that has been home to many undiscovered musicians and artists. Being a musician herself (a pianist to be exact) and going through a quarter-life crisis at the age of 25, Mia who graduated with a business degree is figuring out her life as she's torn between doing the sensible thing by living the life she has planned out with her degree or to follow her one true passion; music. <br><br>But when one <b>Will Ryan</b> crosses path with her and opens up her eyes to a whole new life where music is concerned, she's about to realize that life is about taking chances sometimes and following your heart. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427478435i/14274945.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>Allow me to preface my thoughts by introducing my new book boyfriend:</i>
</b><br><br><b>Will Ryan, oh sweet motha of jeebus that is him.</b> He stole my heart from the first moment he showed up and whipped out a rosary chain! He had such an irresistible charm that had me grinning from ear to ear everytime he burst out into a converation. His love for music comes alive through the pages when he speaks about it with such passion and he was just the most kind-hearted, free-spirited and forgiving guy you can possibly ask for. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427822469i/14324331.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Now Mia really tested my patience with this read. Honestly I nearly DNF-ed this read 2 or 3 times because I was at my breaking point with this woman and the amount of frustration and RAGE boiled up in me was enough to send me into annihilation mode. In my eyes, she was such a hypocritical, judgemental b*tch that couldn't see the most amazing, patient guy standing in front of her and instead decided to f*ck things up with him SEVERAL times. I mean, C'MON!! I would sell my left kidney in a heartbeat to be able to find a guy like Will. <br><br>It broke my heart so many times for Will when Mia couldn't get her shit straight and being absolutely fickled about whether she should reciprocate her feelings for him. It left me feeling so angry at her that I had to put down my read, mentally write a hate note to Mia and take in deep breaths. But it's also at this point where I tried to reason out with myself on why she would act this way. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427821215i/14324226.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And honestly, I'm glad that I did because I found it in myself to forgive her. Often in life, we always wonder if we make the right choices and if opting for a safer route is the right one indeed. People often forget that fear is something that drives us to do unwanted things and it's only when we screwed up is when we learn what truly matters in your life. I can see where Mia is coming from and while I don't approve of her choices sometimes, <i>I get it.</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427478435i/14274945.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>Sweet Thing</u> is a journey of self-discovery filled with ups and downs, joyous and heartbreaking moments, finding friendship in the strangest places and most of all, taking that risk and fall in love. I really struggled with how to rate this one because on one end, it was beautifully written and there was just a certain depth to this read that strike a cord with me. The rich music setting also added another beautiful layer to it and there was just <i>so much</i> you can take away from this read. But on the other end, the choices that Mia made truly left me raging in frustration and made me all stabby. On an angst scale of 1-10, the angst was a very high 9 and I swear I could feel my veins popping during this read. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427821215i/14324227.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>Weighing all the highs &amp; lows of this read and how it affected me emotionally, I'd say it was definitely a solid 4-stars read for me. It's just one of those unforgettable reads that you'll look back and say "oh this book sure as hell did a number on me!" and I don't regret going through a single moment of it. <br><br>I'm not sure how I've missed out on this author previously but she's definitely one to be on a lookout for. Considering this was a debut novel by her, I was captivated by her writing as this read consumed me from the very beginning and by the end of it, I was left in awe on how she brought everything back to a full circle. <br><br>I would recommend if this read if you're a fan of the music-setting read that's (be warned) profoundly heartbreaking yet beautifully thought-provoking as you embark on this journey of self-discovery ♥ <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427478435i/14274945.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i><u>Sweet Thing</u> is a standalone contemporary romance read.</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427351718i/14265304.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><a href="http://readescapadereviews.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427480966i/14275361.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.facebook.com/readingescapadeblog" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427480966i/14275362.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://twitter.com/readingescapade" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427480966i/14275363.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>
