<div id="review_607502002" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/607502002" />
    <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr"><img alt="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1465384674p2/9080319.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/607502002?book_show_action=true">May 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr">Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17609127-sweet-thing">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer607502002" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1218507806901213366">Awesome debut novel! Freaking loved it!<br/><br/><a href='http://photobucket.com/images/Applause%20gifs' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413543ra/814419.gif' alt='Applause gifs photo: applause applause.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>This is the story of Mia and Will. Mia moves from Ann Arbor (shout out to my hometown) Michigan to NYC after her father passes away. On the flight to New York, she sits next to a very hot, very flying-freaked-out Will Ryan. He's got his guitar and a rosary....around his neck. Hmm. They hit it off, chatting comfortably the entire flight. Here is where I fell in love with that man. He was so irresistibly sweet and funny, I couldn't resist. The rosary arou</span>
  <span id="freeText1218507806901213366" style="display:none">Awesome debut novel! Freaking loved it!<br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/Applause%20gifs" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413543ra/814419.gif" alt="Applause gifs photo: applause applause.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This is the story of Mia and Will. Mia moves from Ann Arbor (shout out to my hometown) Michigan to NYC after her father passes away. On the flight to New York, she sits next to a very hot, very flying-freaked-out Will Ryan. He's got his guitar and a rosary....around his neck. Hmm. They hit it off, chatting comfortably the entire flight. Here is where I fell in love with that man. He was so irresistibly sweet and funny, I couldn't resist. The rosary around the neck made me laugh out loud...obviously not a true Catholic as that's balked in Catechism 101. Anyways.....they part ways only after Will insinuating they're soul mates for living through a life threatening event together. Ha. Loved him....oh, I already stated that. <br><br>My Will-<br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Male%20Eye%20Candy/097d38aa8bfc2bb7fd79534755279fef_zps784acfc9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420393i/833935._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 097d38aa8bfc2bb7fd79534755279fef_zps784acfc9.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Mia starts her life in the city. She takes over running her Pop's diner. Her parents were divorced when she was a baby. Her dad was a very eclectic music buff, her mom more conservative and driven career wise. Mia was close to her Pop, even with him 1000 miles away. She had a great support system to help her with the diner. Great friends she would need through the journey that lies ahead. After all, this wasn't her plan when she attended Brown University to own a diner in Manhattan. <br><br>My Mia-<br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Women%20for%20reviews/567491523ad1dbcb07018fa34dee8c74_zps7da67039.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419681i/832357._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 567491523ad1dbcb07018fa34dee8c74_zps7da67039.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Mia runs into Will at the diner. His band is playing in a local bar. She's in search of a roommate. Without much thought, she offers him a room in her apartment. It's very apparent early on that Will is totally enamored with Mia. They both share a love of music. Music is instilled in this entire book. Mia teaches piano and Will plays several instruments (mainly guitar) and the times they come together and play was one of the best parts of the book. They had an easy friendship and Will was just what Mia needed during such a trying time. Music is everything to Will. He's not out for fame and fortune... Just to be able to perform and do what he loves. <br><br>What Will doesn't realize is how set Mia is in her ideals of the kind of life she's going to have. The kind of man she's going to be with. Will doesn't fit that bill....and she pretty blatantly tells him so. It broke his heart time and again. It was obvious she had feelings for him but she just didn't accept him for her future. She saw what happened with her parents...the free spirited artist. He'll either live on pennies or he'll make it big someday and leave her behind. Neither option is a path she's aiming for in life. So she just continues dating douche-bag businessmen right under Will's nose.<br><br><b>“It's a fool who thinks love will set him free. Love equals a morbid and relentless fear of losing the other person” </b><br><br>Mia with Jackson-<br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/image_zps9e708cf4.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420393i/833936.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps9e708cf4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>It broke my heart watching Mia's antics with Will. I wanted to scream at her for being a heartless b&amp;tch but I knew she was human and a product of the life she's lived so far. I was so happy to finally read a book that didn't have tons of emotional "I had a horrible childhood" baggage. She had great parents and they loved her. She just had this ideal and Will didn't measure up....or was her wall something totally different? Was it ideals or was it more? How much rejection will Will take before he gives up and can Mia stand to see him walk away?<br><br><b>“He looked so pathetic standing there, rejected. He corrected himself a couple of times when his body made involuntary movements to reach out and touch me. He was fighting the urge just to simply take my hand or kiss my cheek. I didn’t know why I was being so harsh… The charade and the constant touching created so much confusion. I couldn’t tell anymore what we were to each other.”</b><br><br>This book was a metamorphosis of sorts for Mia. She needed to find herself, to find what was truly important for her in life before she was ready to move forward in a relationship. But can Will's heart hold on that long?<br><br>Loved the character development, the secondary characters, the music, the writing style... Also not one single typo found. I seriously cannot find a weakness in any part of the book. As much as Mia frustrated me, I understood her. I understood what it's like to go to college, have ideals and expect life to fall into this cookie cutter plan you've got set for yourself. Then life happens.....<br><br>On a lighter note, this was one of my favorite early conversations between Will and Mia- <br><b><br>“There are at least five swear words I like better than fuck. My favorites are compound words like apeshit, craphat or batshit, but above all, my numero uno, all-time favorite swear word is assclown, without a doubt. Asshat runs a close second. I must say, very few things give me greater pleasure than calling someone an assclown when they really fit the bill. I love it more than puppies and baby seals.”</b><br><br>At the risk of naming other books in a review, I feel safe listing a couple simply because this is a debut author and her book rivals that of a couple best sellers very similar to it. I felt a big similarity to the whole Thoughtless series in this book. It revolved around music and the heroine was one that I too wanted to strangle (no love triangle though.). It also had Slam poetry and that reminded me of Slammed.<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/image_zps37039b9e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380416809i/823672.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps37039b9e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The Prologue was awesome- different. Loved it. Go forth and read this. You will NOT be disappointed. <br><br><b>“You have to teach your heart and mind how to sing together... then you'll hear the sound of your soul” </b></span>
  <a data-text-id="1218507806901213366" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_598659498" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/598659498" />
    <a title="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog"><img alt="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1429608146p2/12994342.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/598659498?book_show_action=true">Apr 24, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" href="/user/show/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog">Smitten&#39;s Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/18043136-sweet-thing">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=angst-filled-reads">angst-filled-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=emotional-reads">emotional-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=great-surrounding-characters">great-surrounding-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=say-it-with-music">say-it-with-music</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=hea">hea</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=men-with-ink">men-with-ink</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=stand-alone">stand-alone</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=rock-star-hero">rock-star-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=amazing-sexual-tension">amazing-sexual-tension</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer598659498" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14126889178977159781"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391358393i/8377647._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418864i/829762._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Stunning!<br/><br/>Absolutely loved this. It really was gorgeous. <br/><br/>It's a story of friendship, fear, insecurity, loss, self discovery and faith.<br/><br/>I absolutely love those stories where two characters make that transition from friendship to something more. It creates such a warm, fuzzy feeling. And <i>Sweet Thing</i> was no exception.<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Whatever you need me to be, I'll be! Friends? Fine! Best friends? Great! I'll do it, because I want you in my life more than anything I have ever wanted."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>Music plays a huge </span>
  <span id="freeText14126889178977159781" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391358393i/8377647._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418864i/829762._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Stunning!<br><br>Absolutely loved this. It really was gorgeous. <br><br>It's a story of friendship, fear, insecurity, loss, self discovery and faith.<br><br>I absolutely love those stories where two characters make that transition from friendship to something more. It creates such a warm, fuzzy feeling. And <i>Sweet Thing</i> was no exception.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Whatever you need me to be, I'll be! Friends? Fine! Best friends? Great! I'll do it, because I want you in my life more than anything I have ever wanted."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Music plays a huge part in this book. The characters use music to say the words they are unable to speak and to convey emotion that they are unable to explain. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418864i/829763.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Playing, writing, listening. They connect through music, they use music to comfort them, to drown sorrows, to feel closer to those they have lost and to heal. It's incredibly emotive and really gives the reader an insight into the minds and souls of the characters.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Will could dance and if I remember correctly, someone told me once to stay away from a man who could dance.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Will is a fantastic hero. He is cheeky and loveable right from the word go. The author cleverly introduces him to the reader in his most vulnerable state and you instantly fall in love with him. He is cocky and cute, but not too proud or arrogant. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"What do you want to do?" I asked.<br>"I just want to get wasted with you and find out if there is a god," he murmured into my neck before tugging on my earlobe with his teeth.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>The plotline isn't anything off the wall or ground breaking, but the execution and characterisation of Mia and Will are what make this book so beautiful. I was drawn in to their world and I didn't want to climb out.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418864i/829764._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved the feel, created by surrounding characters, the visual of Kell's Cafe, the apartment, Jackson... everything. Renee has a way of writing you <i>into</i> the story.<br><br>Some parts of this book are almost painful to read. I was tearing my hair out and wanted to scream at Mia, at times. But she comes with her own set of heavy issues and the story is true to those in the way Mia reacts to things.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>It's the only way to know you're really in love, when you ask the question would it be harder to watch him die, or to know he'll watch me die? Is there more mercy in being the one who does the watching or in being the one who does the dying? It's when you realize what mercy-killing actually means, it's when you actually care to the point of tormenting worry. It's not roses and white horses, it's fucking brutal and it can send a person running for the hills. To love is brave and Will was the bravest person I knew.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>My heart shattered for Will, sooo many times. He was just too adorable. He was so constant and, supportive, and sweet, and... *sigh*. Girls, you <i>will</i> adore Wilbur Ryan!<br><br>This is a very quick, easy read. I read it in one go and felt like it was over in a flash. But it was perfect. It was long enough to build and run with the story, but not too long that there were unnecessary fillers or parts that dragged.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Wilbur, I want to have like a million of your babies."<br>He looked happier than I had ever seen him.<br>"Really? Should we start now?"<br>"Definitely."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>And can I just end by saying, at the end of this book, the author writes...<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>For Jackson: The best damn dog in the world. RIP, Buddy.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Oh my goodness. Cue me = blubbering wreck! *sob*<br><br>So anyway, this book has been getting fantastic reviews all over the place, and I can totally see why. If you've got it on your TBR list and are umming and arring, or don't know what to read next, give <i>Sweet Thing</i> a go. It's got a bit of everything, from cute, to sexy, from dark, to light. I loved it and would highly recommend. And I do believe it's on sale right now!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418864i/829765._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b><i>Sweet Thing</i> Statistics</b><br><b>Length</b>: 342 pages<br><b>Steam Rating (out of 5):</b> ♥♥♥<br><b>Ending:</b> HEA<br><b>Series:</b> ✗ <br><b>Can this be read as a standalone?</b> Yes<br><b>Themes:</b><br>Music<br>Grief<br>Friendship<br><b>Warning. This book includes...</b> <br>Death of a dog<br><b>Writing:</b> Great<br><br><b>AMAZON UK:</b> <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.co.uk/Sweet-Thing-ebook/dp/B00BSY916G/ref=sr_1_1?ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1370857560&amp;sr=8-1&amp;keywords=sweet+thing+by+renee+carlino">http://www.amazon.co.uk/Sweet-Thing-e...</a><br><b>AMAZON US:</b> <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.com/Sweet-Thing-ebook/dp/B00BSY916G/ref=sr_1_1?ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1370857560&amp;sr=8-1&amp;keywords=sweet+thing+by+renee+carlino">http://www.amazon.com/Sweet-Thing-ebo...</a><br><br><b>
  <i>Like This Review...?</i>
</b><br>To read more reviews go to my Book Blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/">http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/</a><br>Follow me on Twitter: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://twitter.com/SmittenSC">https://twitter.com/SmittenSC</a><br>Find me on Pinterest: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://pinterest.com/smittensc/">http://pinterest.com/smittensc/</a><br>Join in the fun on Facebook: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/SmittensBookBlog">https://www.facebook.com/SmittensBook...</a></span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1309255834" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1309255834" />
    <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli"><img alt="Pearl Angeli" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1588420465p2/31514572.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1309255834?book_show_action=true">Jun 16, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pearl Angeli" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli">Pearl Angeli</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781476763934" href="/book/show/18280761-sweet-thing">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=owned-physical-copy">owned-physical-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=hot-male-characters">hot-male-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=new-adult-contemporary">new-adult-contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=annoying-heroines">annoying-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=2015-reads">2015-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1309255834" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer229679484227534418"><i>
  <b>"You have to teach your heart and mind how to sing together... Then you'll hear the sound of your soul."</b>
</i> <br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18334246.Sweet_Thing__Sweet_Thing___1_' title='Sweet Thing (Sweet Thing, #1) by Renee Carlino' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sweet Thing</a> is indeed a sweet thing. I love the musical theme. It kind of makes me feel comforted. Actually, the theme was particularly the main reason why I took this book in the first place. It holds such delightful promises.<br/><br/>The book opens when <b>Mia Kelly's</b> dad died and she had to move on by going to New York to settle and find herself-- discover her dreams and perhaps find her dream man</span>
  <span id="freeText229679484227534418" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>"You have to teach your heart and mind how to sing together... Then you'll hear the sound of your soul."</b>
</i> <br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18334246.Sweet_Thing__Sweet_Thing___1_" title="Sweet Thing (Sweet Thing, #1) by Renee Carlino" rel="nofollow noopener">Sweet Thing</a> is indeed a sweet thing. I love the musical theme. It kind of makes me feel comforted. Actually, the theme was particularly the main reason why I took this book in the first place. It holds such delightful promises.<br /><br />The book opens when <b>Mia Kelly's</b> dad died and she had to move on by going to New York to settle and find herself-- discover her dreams and perhaps find her dream man. While on the way, she met the handsome and struggling musician <b>Will</b> whom she instantly felt a strange connection with. Because Will is such a funny, cool, and sprightly guy, and because Mia has that musical inclination as well, she was not able to resist her attraction towards him. They met again for the second time and Mia learned that Will was in need of a room to stay while he's working at a bar. They eventually ended up as roommates.<br /><br />I enjoyed most parts of this book. I especially love the way both characters connected through their music. Will playing a guitar and singing, and Mia playing a piano. Don't they really make a good pair? *sigh*. And Will... Will... Will... What a perfect guy he is. If he exists in real life, then I'll definitely take him home. Ha! He has such a great and deep soul, one who's always there to stay by your side whenever you need someone to rely on, and one who overlooks your imperfections and just focuses on your beautiful side just to be with you. <br /><br />What kept me from rating this book higher was <b>Mia</b>. I understand her angst, but I could not understand how inconsistent she was in this book when it came to her decisions and her reasons. She made a slightly bad impression when she underestimated Will and his not-promising musical career and instantly hooked up with a rich, handsome, and boring banker instead-- without even getting to know the guy better. For me, it was such a crazy resolve. Then she ended up being jealous becuase of Will's series of girlfriends.<br /><br />Female leads with immature attitude doesn't always sit well with me. That includes Mia. All throughout the book I was so hoping that her character will improve, but nah. Maybe improved a little but still, her confused mind and the way she continued to reject Will kind of annoyed me. Like, please can you just love Will already? He's proved so much and yet.... argh. (I'm already ranting. Haha!)<br /><br />Anyways, despite Mia's attitude, I still find this book good. I also highly recommend this, because the concept is awesome and it's not often done. Only rare authors give this theme a chance. The romance was good and there were steamy scenes, too. Are you a fan of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5430144.Colleen_Hoover" title="Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Colleen Hoover</a>'s <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17788403.Maybe_Someday__Maybe___1_" title="Maybe Someday (Maybe, #1) by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Maybe Someday</a>? Then go read this book! :)<br /><br />Rating: 3 Stars</span>
  <a data-text-id="229679484227534418" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText15679038513652301348" style="display:none"><b>A Million Stars!!! This book was amazing!!! In the top 5 books I have read this year!!! Such a beautiful story. This book didn't appeal to me when it first came out for some reason. I only read it because my buddy reader wanted to read it and let me tell you I am so glad I did. I laughed, I cried and I just loved this book to pieces. I am normally one who has to have steam in her books. This book wasn't that steamy but that was okay. The story was so good that it truly didn't matter. When the couple finally got together it wasn't about steamy sex it was about making love and it was beautiful. This truly is an excellent book. I would recommend it to anyone looking for a beautiful love story. A must read. </b></span>

<div id="review_606595955" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/606595955" />
    <a title="Renee" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12732363-renee"><img alt="Renee" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1596939182p2/12732363.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/606595955?book_show_action=true">May 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Renee" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Renee" href="/user/show/12732363-renee">Renee</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17609127-sweet-thing">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12732363-renee?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12732363-renee?shelf=reread">reread</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12732363-renee?shelf=best-books-of-all-time">best-books-of-all-time</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12732363-renee?shelf=6-star-rating-loved-it-rare-epic">6-star-rating-loved-it-rare-epic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12732363-renee?shelf=angsty">angsty</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer606595955" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7044057721058574223"><b>
  <i> One of the <u>BEST</u> books I have read all year!!!!</i>
</b><br/><br/><b>SPOILER-FREE REVIEW!!!</b><br/><br/><b>******* 6 SWEET SEXY STARS ********</b><br/><br/><i>
  <b>A-M-A-Z-I-N-G!!</b>
</i> I completely <i>**loved**adored**</i> this musical love story! This book was so beautifully written. The writing was raw, rhythmic, poetic and I found myself continuously moved by the inspirational dialogue. I felt like I wanted to recite the entire book in my status updates...<br/><br/>I think most us as woman whether single, a wife or a mother; at some point in our lives ask ourselves</span>
  <span id="freeText7044057721058574223" style="display:none"><b>
  <i> One of the <u>BEST</u> books I have read all year!!!!</i>
</b><br><br><b>SPOILER-FREE REVIEW!!!</b><br><br><b>******* 6 SWEET SEXY STARS ********</b><br><br><i>
  <b>A-M-A-Z-I-N-G!!</b>
</i> I completely <i>**loved**adored**</i> this musical love story! This book was so beautifully written. The writing was raw, rhythmic, poetic and I found myself continuously moved by the inspirational dialogue. I felt like I wanted to recite the entire book in my status updates...<br><br>I think most us as woman whether single, a wife or a mother; at some point in our lives ask ourselves if we have made the right choices. Some look at their lives and think <i>"How could I have been so stupid? How did I get here? Why didn't I choose a different path?</i> Others try protect themselves and end up opting for the "safer option". It's human nature to question our choices but so many times fear gets in the way of our choices. Fear is an manipulating evil. No body can tell you which choices to make, it's simpy a lesson one must learn on their own. To me, this book is about discovery, friendship, taking chances forgiveness and love.<br><br><br><i>
  <b>“Wisdom is not the same as information; it's something entirely different. It's often mistaken as good advise, but wisdom cannot be imparted to someone. Wisdom can only be earned; it's a by-product of experience, not necessarily knowledge.”</b>
</i><br><br><br><br>As most of you know, I don't like to give away too much about a story in my reviews. I believe that when your reading a book there should be a sense of mystery. Where's the joy in reading a book and knowing what's going to happen. It's like opening beautifully wrapped present but already knowing what's inside - it's pointless!So I'm going to try my best to provide you with a spoiler free review.<br> <br><br><i>
  <b>Will</b>
</i> is a 29 year old sexy, spontaneous, witty, easy going <i>*hot*</i> musician on the way to making it big. I was in love with his honesty and integrity and with the way he continued to be in Mia's life regardless of the hurt it caused. My heart shattered for him over and over again and there was point where I felt didn't think I could read on...so glad I did though! I loved Will to bits, <b><i>not to mention I wanted to push him against the wall, rip his clothes off and ... and ....</i> too much right??!!! </b><br><br><u>
  <b>Will </b>
</u><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/photos/1369012668p8/765605.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>
  <b>“You have to teach your heart and mind how to sing together... then you'll hear the sound of your soul”.</b>
</i><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/photos/1369012590p8/765604.jpg" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>
  <b>Mia</b>
</i> is a 25 year old who is on the road to discovery. She makes a lot of mistakes along the way but that also makes her character realistic. Although, there were many, many, <i>
  <b>many</b>
</i> times I wanted to beat the shit out her – she's a was likeable character but it was time for her to literally <i> face the music!</i> <br><br><b>
  <u>Mia</u>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/photos/1369024479p8/765701.jpg" width="250" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>
  <i>“Just let me kiss your mouth”. ~ Will</i>
</b><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/photos/1369012696p8/765609.jpg" width="250" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>
  <b>“It's a fool who thinks love will set him free. Love equals a morbid and relentless fear of losing the other person.. It’s not roses and white horses, it’s fucking brutal and it can send a person running for the hills. To love is brave...”</b>
</i><br><br><br>(I <i>**heart**</i> that quote!)<br> <br><br>I also ***LOVED*** the author, Renee Carlio's reference to one of my all time favorite lebanese poets, <i>
  <b>Khalil Gebran</b>
</i> who wrote the book <b>
  <u>The Prophet</u>
</b>. (Yay to lebs!!!.. That was a BIG **Squeeee*** moment for me!) I also found myself constantly searching the songs that were mentioned throughout the book - it was an awesome music list!<br><br>This whole year I've been reading books and feeling like something is seriously missing. Sure, there have been books I've rated 5 stars and I have enjoyed, but they were missing something and for the life of me I couldn't pin point what it was. After reading the <i>
  <b>Sweet Thing</b>
</i> - I know what was <i>missing</i>. What was missing was <i>heart!</i> This book touches your heart to the very core.. this book right here is what pulled me out of my book slump. I felt completely connected this book and the characters. It's books like these that stem my **love** of reading<br><br><i>Maryse</i> is one my favorite bloggers. I was so excited to see the author, Renee Carlino had mentioned her in the book. I think Maryse hit the nail on the head in her review on this book. She said <b>
  <i>“This is what I’ve been craving, waiting for… wanting, needing to read for weeks. Months. This was it. This was the one I was referring to, when I would bemoan that I wished I could find another book that would make me crazy for it. This one had that feeling. The feeling that all of my favorite books gave me, all wrapped into one.”.</i>
</b><br><br>What better way to describe it people than it gives you <i>
  <b>"That feeling"!!!!</b>
</i><br><br><br><i>
  <b>Renee Carlino</b>
</i> <i>(Great name by the way!)</i> is a soulful, wise and talented author who has given us a piece of her heart through a beautiful love story. Not only is she incredibly talented and has a great name but check her out people.. The woman's a stunner! She looks exactly like <i>
  <u>Monica Bellucci</u>
</i>...<i>
  <b>Total hot mama! </b>
</i> Can't wait to read more of her work!<br><br>If you loved the books <i>
  <b>Thoughtless</b>
</i> and <i>
  <b>How to Kill a Rockstar</b>
</i> (which I loved) you will absolutely love <b>
  <u>Sweet Thing!</u>
</b> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/photos/1369012380p8/765602.jpg" width="320" height="320" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <br><b>***BONUS MATERIAL****Renee Carlino's additional material in <i>Will's POV (TWO DIFFERENT SCENES)</i>*** </b><br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.maryse.net/news/sweet-thing-by-renee-carlino-is-only-0-99-cents-right-now-plus-i-have-a-special-scene-from-wills-pov.html">http://www.maryse.net/news/sweet-thin...</a><br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://aestasbookblog.com/book-review-sweet-thing-renee-carlino/">http://aestasbookblog.com/book-review...</a><br><br><br>I would recommend this book to anyone who wants <i>"That feeling" </i>back! That feeling when you can't stop thinking about a book and keep checking the time to see when you can start reading it again. That feeling when your partner needs to physically pry the book from your hands at 2 am in the morning and kick your ass to bed - and then you <i>(Me)</i> downloads the kindle app on your iPhone while in bed, quitely turns the brightness setting on your phone down, holds your breath and hopes to God your husband doesn't catch you reading again. Lastly, that feeling when you have finally finished the book, you cannot stop thinking about it for days after and you can't wait to read it again! If you want <i>"that feeling"</i> friends.. then this here is the book for you!!!<br><br><br><i>
  <b>“I stood offstage in the shadows, completely absorbed by the sound, where I decided that playing the guitar should be a prerequisite for manhood”.</b>
</i><br><br><br><i>Besides Ladies.... who can resist a hot sexy man that can play the guitar, piano AND sing... <b>I know I can't... *WINK*</b></i> </span>
  <a data-text-id="7044057721058574223" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer636245747" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14760419648865048588"><b>And the award for the most disappointing and bitchy character goes to…. Mia Kelly!</b><br/><br/>Mia; main character and narrator; is super judgmental, hypocritical, snob, dishonest, self-centered, self-pitying, rude and cruel when angry. She is the worst. I wonder how someone who prides herself in being sensible could make such stupid life decisions and behaved so terrible to loved ones. I truly could not stand her and there were plenty of moments when I considered simply DNFing this novel.<br/><br/>It is very likely t</span>
  <span id="freeText14760419648865048588" style="display:none"><b>And the award for the most disappointing and bitchy character goes to…. Mia Kelly!</b><br /><br />Mia; main character and narrator; is super judgmental, hypocritical, snob, dishonest, self-centered, self-pitying, rude and cruel when angry. She is the worst. I wonder how someone who prides herself in being sensible could make such stupid life decisions and behaved so terrible to loved ones. I truly could not stand her and there were plenty of moments when I considered simply DNFing this novel.<br /><br />It is very likely that my huge issues with heroine played a role but either way I truly did not like this book. Overall flow of the story was weird and storytelling was extremely weak. Not recommended!<br /><br />MORE REVIEWS ON MY BLOG <a href="http://readingismybreathing.blogspot.cz/" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2414760942" />
    <a title="Aj the Ravenous Reader" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader"><img alt="Aj the Ravenous Reader" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1557800982p2/30248594.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2414760942?book_show_action=true">Jun 05, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aj the Ravenous Reader" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aj the Ravenous Reader" href="/user/show/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader">Aj the Ravenous Reader</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/36082176-sweet-thing">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader?shelf=definitely-not-young-adult">definitely-not-young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader?shelf=physically-owned-books">physically-owned-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2414760942" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4736114056864232472"><br/>It was a quite a struggle to read a story in the POV of a character I strongly disliked at first. If it weren’t for <b>Will</b>, I wouldn’t have had the patience to read it through but he is such a great, sweet, talented and genuinely thoughtful guy that I needed to know more about him even if it had to be through <b>Mia</b>’s too self-absorbed, self-serving and arrogant mind. I couldn’t fully blame her though. It’s probably just the grief and uncertainty about herself. <br/><br/>I guess she needed more time and experi</span>
  <span id="freeText4736114056864232472" style="display:none"><br />It was a quite a struggle to read a story in the POV of a character I strongly disliked at first. If it weren’t for <b>Will</b>, I wouldn’t have had the patience to read it through but he is such a great, sweet, talented and genuinely thoughtful guy that I needed to know more about him even if it had to be through <b>Mia</b>’s too self-absorbed, self-serving and arrogant mind. I couldn’t fully blame her though. It’s probably just the grief and uncertainty about herself. <br /><br />I guess she needed more time and experience to realize that love and stability aren’t the same thing. You don’t look for a person with a stable career and force yourself to fall in love with him. Instead, you fall in love with a person and try to build a secure and comfortable life with him. <br /><br />Thank goodness, Mia finally realized the error of her ways in the last quarter of the novel and was punished enough for her to deserve a happy ending. I was actually really pissed at the angst and heartbreaks both characters willingly subjected their hearts to, to the point of making me think their relationship was borderline toxic until I understood that they needed to go through the pain to discover who they were and what they truly meant for each other. <br /><br />There was just times the narrative got a little repetitive, also kind of a sexually too graphic but still enjoyable and gripping enough for me to read it in one day. What I liked about the story is the great supporting characters and the concept of the small café with poetry reading nights as well as the element of music. In short, for a New Adult novel, this wasn’t that bad. Lol.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4736114056864232472" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_589938584" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/589938584" />
    <a title="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16496589-jx-pinklady-reviews-bookwormthoughts"><img alt="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591195447p2/16496589.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/589938584?book_show_action=true">Apr 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" href="/user/show/16496589-jx-pinklady-reviews-bookwormthoughts">Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17609127-sweet-thing">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer589938584" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12218001244130121403"><a href='http://s1326.photobucket.com/user/w8tman7/media/0384ffc7-522a-4554-8b89-a4a9e07950b1_zpsc8424765.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417573i/826098._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo 0384ffc7-522a-4554-8b89-a4a9e07950b1_zpsc8424765.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>**May contain small spoilers**<br/><br/><a href='http://s1326.photobucket.com/user/w8tman7/media/4f93f8d8-e7a1-4ad8-a2e8-7732e6041cd3_zpscac0d0dc.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417573i/826099._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo 4f93f8d8-e7a1-4ad8-a2e8-7732e6041cd3_zpscac0d0dc.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>After her beloved father's sudden death Mia finds herself on a plane to New York where she slips right into her Pops old life; she runs his cafe, loves his eclectic mix of friends and makes a special, new musician friend of her very own....Introducing the very charming, very lovely, nearly 30 years old, scared of flying, I can play any instrument, <i>
  <b>Will Ryan ♥</b>
</i><br/><br/><i>
  <b>"....brown dishevelled hair and dark eyes, a chiselled jaw, high cheekbones, and great lips"</b>
</i><br/><i>"</i></span>
  <span id="freeText12218001244130121403" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1326.photobucket.com/user/w8tman7/media/0384ffc7-522a-4554-8b89-a4a9e07950b1_zpsc8424765.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417573i/826098._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 0384ffc7-522a-4554-8b89-a4a9e07950b1_zpsc8424765.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>**May contain small spoilers**<br><br><a href="http://s1326.photobucket.com/user/w8tman7/media/4f93f8d8-e7a1-4ad8-a2e8-7732e6041cd3_zpscac0d0dc.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417573i/826099._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 4f93f8d8-e7a1-4ad8-a2e8-7732e6041cd3_zpscac0d0dc.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>After her beloved father's sudden death Mia finds herself on a plane to New York where she slips right into her Pops old life; she runs his cafe, loves his eclectic mix of friends and makes a special, new musician friend of her very own....Introducing the very charming, very lovely, nearly 30 years old, scared of flying, I can play any instrument, <i>
  <b>Will Ryan ♥</b>
</i><br><br><i>
  <b>"....brown dishevelled hair and dark eyes, a chiselled jaw, high cheekbones, and great lips"</b>
</i><br><i>"....kind, sensitive, creative, determined"</i><br><blockquote>
  <i>♥"Your antics are cute, Will." ♥</i>
</blockquote> Cute and adorable, Wilbur (yes that's his real name!) sits next to Mia on her flight to New York (♥ fate is amazing ♥) Mia is his flight distraction; they have the same 'cool' taste in music. <br><br>Their personalities draw each other together.<br> <br><i>"We kind of hit it off.......there was something about him that drew me in....."</i><br><b>
  <i>but</i>
</b><br><i>".....I convinced myself at that moment that Will was not boyfriend material..."</i> <br><br>And here the <i>
  <b>frustration</b>
</i> began....aghhhh!! Mia!!!! What's wrong with you? Will is adorable, caring, gorgeous....just perfect!!! She sees him as a struggling musician; she <u>should</u> trust him, he has dreams and talent....a sense of truth and faith ♥<br><a href="http://s1326.photobucket.com/user/w8tman7/media/c10389c6-e019-4949-9e0d-c63983cd48ff_zps8e57dca6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417573i/826101._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo c10389c6-e019-4949-9e0d-c63983cd48ff_zps8e57dca6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>"...I felt like I had known him forever."</i>
</b><br><br>So Mia &amp; Will become 'roomies' &amp; the very best of friends but should they be more? Mia pushes Will away into the arms of another....then she is jealous??? But still she thinks they should only be friends; best, best friends, forever in your life kind of a friend. Why didn't she tell him she was free and single....why??<br><br><i>
  <b>"...I knew Will would eventually move on."</b>
</i> That was her fear. It made me feel achingly sad inside, if Mia would just open up to him, reach out, he would be everything she needed him to be and more, I just knew it...<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I had no desire to be his humdrum history......it took every fibre of my being to refuse his touch in that way."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>Mia loves Will but is scared of his outlook to life, his free and easy spirit. She would rather be his <i>friend</i> in his present and future, than a <i>lover</i> of his past. I believe her parent's past relationship has an effect on Mia's judgement in this situation. The author cleverly interweaves two love stories, her parents and of course, Will &amp; Mia, both stories had me in tears at times. ♥<br><br><b>"Love life and life will love you back"</b>~ Pops <br>Pops would have loved Will - her mum and dad's belief systems are pulling her in different directions.<br><br>Will is an amazingly talented musician and writer, Mia herself is talented in this area and together they share their passion and love for music. But Mia knows that Will is on the brink of something special.<br><a href="http://s1326.photobucket.com/user/w8tman7/media/roflbot_zpse114430c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417573i/826102._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo roflbot_zpse114430c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=gMY4W0l4peY">http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=gMY4W0...</a><br>These three lines from an old Smiths song perfectly sums up their relationship for a large part of the story, take a listen, it's a fabulous song, I think so anyway.....<br><br><i>
  <b>"And so it began my secret and suppressed obsession with the sensitive, tortured, artist soul."</b>
</i><br><br><i>
  <b>"I wanted to commit everything about Will to memory before I lost him..." <br><br>"I cried because I knew that if I gave myself to Will, I would be left in pieces... left behind. The only way I could hang on was to be his friend, even though every part of me wanted more." <br><br>"I was drowning in a huge chasm created by some obsession I have with getting things right."</b>
</i><br><br><i>"You're beautiful and amazing and you have a special soul, Mia. You deserve the best."</i><br><b>"You're so good and you don't even know it. Night, Baby." </b>♥<br><br>She breaks his heart.....<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417573i/826104.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>"The leap of faith is giving it a chance and not projecting your own crap on someone else because you're afraid of failing."</i>
</b> <br><br>I really liked the narration. I felt like Mia was talking to me, drawing me into her confidence, her inner feelings. Yes she's extremely frustrating but she has real motivation for her actions...<br><br>'Sweet Thing' doesn't offer instant gratification but a slow build up of character realisation, an intense friendship, a shared love of music and then love of each other. They have a deep, amazing connection...I felt it, it moved me deeply, and left me feeling quite emotional. The extra scenes from Will's POV are a must for 'Will lovers' especially the one at their friends wedding, it had me in tears. Did I mention, I love Will?♥ Money and fame are not his driving force....it is his love and his passion for music and being true to yourself.....Swooooon!!<br><br><b>
  <i>"You're my best f*cking friend, Mia. I wish it were more and I think you know that....Whatever you need me to be, I'll be!"</i>
</b><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <i>"I hadn't believed that people could be made for each other until that moment. "I love you."</i>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><i>
  <b>"We're the static in the chaos, the one thing...the something so sweet."</b>
</i><br><br><u>Share Your Coffee</u><br><i>Share your words<br>Share your music<br>Share you love, your passion, your fears<br>Your hopes, and your dreams<br>Share your precious heart<br>Share your wild mind<br>Share your special soul with me<br>and I promise to<br>give you all mine</i> <br><br>**BR with the very lovely, pink ladies**<br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8843319568517826543">God, I really loved this book!! It's everything a romance book should be and then some. It's hard to believe that this is a debut novel. Renee Carlino is one talented writer and her next book will be an auto-buy for me. <br/><br/>Read it for the romance, read it for the music (music plays a huge part in this story), or read it for the excellent writing. Just read it!!!</span>

  <span id="freeText12452106463584711645" style="display:none"> <b>^^^3.5 <u>SEXY WILBUR STARS</u>^^^</b><br><br><i>He had a big, thick angel wing tattoo on his forearm....VERY SEXY</i><br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://www.imagechef.com/ic/word_mosaic/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417572i/826091.gif" alt="ImageChef Word Mosaic - ImageChef.com" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </a><br><br>*******************************************************<br>This book starts out with Mia and Will on the airplane headed to New York where both are making a fresh start in their lives. Mia's father passed away and she's taking over her father's business and apartment. Will, a hot musician has no where to go and becomes Mia's ROOMY.<br>Yes....exactly what you think is going to happen...only it took 75% of the book for the two of them to admit their feelings. I really LOVED Will...he was AMAZING, PERFECT, HOT, SWEET, did i say he was perfect???<br>Mia...i wanted to like her, i really did, but not until the end of the book, which THANK YOU MOTHER OF GOD had a Happily Ever After. <br>*******************************************************<br><br><b>"You're name is Wilbur?"</b><br><br><br><b>

<div id="review_2261955263" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2261955263" />
    <a title="Ninoska Goris" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/52598215-ninoska-goris"><img alt="Ninoska Goris" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1578758582p2/52598215.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2261955263?book_show_action=true">Jan 22, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ninoska Goris" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ninoska Goris" href="/user/show/52598215-ninoska-goris">Ninoska Goris</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52598215-ninoska-goris?shelf=2018">2018</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2261955263" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7086655741119974235">English - Español<br/><br/>Will is the almost perfect man that every romantic woman can desire. On the other hand, Mia is the annoyance, interested one. Think that the only way to be happy is to have economic stability. The whole book is spent worshiping Will, but doing all sorts of slights.<br/><br/>Mia must abandon her career and her plans when her biological father dies and moves to New York to the apartment she inherited from her father and take care of the coffeeshop he had. She decides to look for someone to </span>
  <span id="freeText7086655741119974235" style="display:none">English - Español<br /><br />Will is the almost perfect man that every romantic woman can desire. On the other hand, Mia is the annoyance, interested one. Think that the only way to be happy is to have economic stability. The whole book is spent worshiping Will, but doing all sorts of slights.<br /><br />Mia must abandon her career and her plans when her biological father dies and moves to New York to the apartment she inherited from her father and take care of the coffeeshop he had. She decides to look for someone to rent a room and reluctantly offers it to Will, whom she meets on her trip to New York, with the only condition that they will only be friends.<br /><br />It is obvious from the beginning that they have a lot of chemistry and something that unites them deeply: music. But although Mia likes Will, he does not represent the ideals she considers for a couple, among which the most important ones are that be successful and wealthy. Because of this and because she also finds him attractive, she ends up dating Robert, VP at JP Morgan but without any other quality.<br /><br />The outcome seems to me obviously rushed and I did not like that the author include Lauren, a character that has nothing to do with the story, at the beginning and end of the book, just to try to close it with gold clasps and have a "serendipiti" vibe. <br /><br />✨✨✨<br /><br />Will es el hombre casi perfecto que toda mujer romántica pueda desear. Por otro lado, Mia es un incordio, una interesada. Piensa que la única manera de ser feliz es tener estabilidad económica. Se pasa todo el libro adorando a Will, pero haciéndole todo tipo de desaires.<br /><br />Mia debe abandonar su carrera y sus planes cuando su padre biológico muere y se muda a New York al apto que heredó de su padre y hacerse cargo del café que tenía. Decide buscar a quien rentarle una habitación y de mala gana se la ofrece a Will, a quien conoce en su viaje a New York, poniendo como única condición que solo serán amigos. <br /><br />Es obvio desde el inicio que tienen mucha química y algo que los une profundamente: la música. Pero aunque a Mia le gusta Will este no representa los ideales que considera para una pareja, entre los cuales los más importantes son que sea exitoso y adinerado. Por esto y porque además lo encuentra atractivo termina saliendo con Robert, VP en JP Morgan pero sin ninguna otra cualidad. <br /><br />El desenlace me parece a todas luces apresurado y no me gustó que incluyeran a Lauren, un personaje que nada tiene que ver con la historia, al principio y al final del libro, solo para tratar de cerrarlo con broches de oro y tener una vibra "serendipiti". <br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7086655741119974235" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

I am so happy she did.<br/><br/>This book consumed me to the very core. I can not think of a life of a book with out these two characters. They had me wrapped up as their own personal sock puppet just getting hungry with each page wanting more. <br/><br/>Lets meet the cast shall we???<br/><br/><br/><br/><b> Meet MY Will </b> <br/><br/><a href='http://s1321.photobucket.com/user/ambersreadingroom/media/9806C4FA-EB4C-4D04-BF5F-25153E5D51EA-1725-000001CC70DC73BC_zpsaa9dc616.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

  <span id="freeText5303042445605494656" style="display:none">Spoiler Free <br><br><b> 5+++ Beautiful, heart wrenching, outstanding stars!!! </b><br><br>First let me say I am so thankful to the Author for contacting me wanting me to read her book. I am so happy she did.<br><br>This book consumed me to the very core. I can not think of a life of a book with out these two characters. They had me wrapped up as their own personal sock puppet just getting hungry with each page wanting more. <br><br>Lets meet the cast shall we???<br><br><br><br><b> Meet MY Will </b> <br><br><a href="http://s1321.photobucket.com/user/ambersreadingroom/media/9806C4FA-EB4C-4D04-BF5F-25153E5D51EA-1725-000001CC70DC73BC_zpsaa9dc616.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414974i/818766.jpg" alt=" photo 9806C4FA-EB4C-4D04-BF5F-25153E5D51EA-1725-000001CC70DC73BC_zpsaa9dc616.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Will, has made it to my list of book boyfriends. He is right up there with my favorites now. I am so happy to have him on my on growing list. I will re visit him again I am sure. <br><br><b> I wanted to wrap him up in a blanket and put him in my pocket for safekeeping. </b> <br><br>I am just grinning ear to ear thinking about Will. Will, is poetic, spontaneous, and on the brink of fame. The love he has for his music shows in the book and the way both characters bond over it. I could lay there for hours and watch and listen to him sing and play his soul out in front of you. <br><br><b> Mia </b> <br><br><br>Mia is a very likable. You feel every emotion she has and the reasoning behind them. You get captured in her head and still want to scream at her for the obvious reasons. <br><br>How can you not love a book that takes you on such a beautiful journey that captures you and holds you very dearly to its heart. This emotional roller coaster of a ride is one I want to go through all over again to experience it for the first time. <br><br>This is a must read if you love having your heart open on a sleeve for this book to come and jump right open inside of it. If you have the love for music, laughing at the friendships that you see and desperately want to be apart of then this is a must read. <br><br><i> I recived an ARC from the Author exchange for a honest review </i> <br><br><a href="http://www.ambersreadingroom.com" rel="nofollow noopener">My blog Amber's Reading Room for more reviews</a><br><br><a href="http://www.facebook.com/AmbersReadingRoom" rel="nofollow noopener">Like my Facebook blog page</a></span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer594407478" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer3651745980460108803">4 - 4.5 ★'s <br/><blockquote>
  <b>"You have to teach your heart and mind how to sing together... then you'll hear the sound of your soul."<b></b></b>
</blockquote><br/>Mia and Will meet on a plane heading to New York. Her father just passed away and she's going there to run his cafe. Will lives there. He's freaked out about flying and she takes him mind off it. They part ways at the airport thinking that's the end of it but luckily, it's not. <br/><br/>One thing leads to another and Will ends up being Mia's roommate but she's quick to enforce the frien</span>
  <span id="freeText3651745980460108803" style="display:none">4 - 4.5 ★'s <br><blockquote>
  <b>"You have to teach your heart and mind how to sing together... then you'll hear the sound of your soul."<b></b></b>
</blockquote><br>Mia and Will meet on a plane heading to New York. Her father just passed away and she's going there to run his cafe. Will lives there. He's freaked out about flying and she takes him mind off it. They part ways at the airport thinking that's the end of it but luckily, it's not. <br><br>One thing leads to another and Will ends up being Mia's roommate but she's quick to enforce the friends only rule much to Will's dismay. Things get a little dicey when Mia starts dating someone else and Will walks in on them. He <i>has</i> to give Mia a taste of her own medicine but what in the hell was up with the horsie ride? That was just weird. <br><br>Will and Mia are both musicians and I love their love of music and how much they can relate to each other through it. But Mia's father was also a musician and it caused problems between him and her mother leading them to break up. This is something Mia wants to avoid at all costs. She wants a man with a well paying job and Will is not him. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1486678395ra/21940384.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Mia has a lot of maturing to do...not so much about growing up but learning to live <i>her</i> life. She's stuck - not only with her "planned" partner but with dealing with some hard knocks life has given her already. <br><br>After some drama and after a lot of grieving, she <i>wo</i>mans up and decides to put some things to rest so she can move on. She takes some chances and it pays off but...the biggest thing she has to do is be patient. <br><br>I really enjoyed Will and Mia together and the drama was pretty angsty. I did like the way it ended but felt like I needed more happy times. Imagine my surprise in learning that the follow up novella, <i>Sweet Little Thing</i> does just that...and in Will's POV!<br><br><br><i>(Prior to review...)</i><br><b>5/27/13 ~ Will's POV:<br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.maryse.net/news/sweet-thing-by-renee-carlino-is-only-0-99-cents-right-now-plus-i-have-a-special-scene-from-wills-pov.html#more-31979">http://www.maryse.net/news/sweet-thin...</a></b></span>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText4625994100805154245" style="display:none"><b>4,5 Amazing Stars. </b>	<br><br>Mia is heartbroken and lost after her father’s death, so she decides to move to NY and take over his bar. But at the same time life keeps them apart until they figure out what they want and how far they want to go in order to find peace and happiness. <br>Unfortunately, that’s a road that isn’t easy to make and they will have several obstacles, their doubts and ghosts the biggest ones of them, until they finally reach that place. <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394213076ra/8822753.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I loved how music was a big part in this book. She was a complete bitch at several moments and said some really hurtful things. Most of their problems and drama would be nonexistent if she wasn’t like that. <div id="review_607608946" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/607608946" />
    <a title="M. ~ B&amp;B" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14479657-m-b-b"><img alt="M. ~ B&amp;B" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1435261660p2/14479657.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/607608946?book_show_action=true">May 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="M. ~ B&amp;B" class="user" itemprop="url" name="M. ~ B&amp;B" href="/user/show/14479657-m-b-b">M. ~ B&amp;B</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17609127-sweet-thing">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer607608946" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5673589994783204783"><b>
  <i>I remember the journey that brought me to those decisions and that memory gives me great solace, because the memory is a reminder of who I am among all the chaos that is life.</i>
</b><br/><br/>I am very torn about this book. It started out as a four star for me, then almost became a DNF, changed into three star, back to almost DNF and ended with four star. It has been the hardest book for me to finish. I've read disturbing books, crappy books and just boring books and none of them gave me as much of a hard ti</span>
  <span id="freeText5673589994783204783" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>I remember the journey that brought me to those decisions and that memory gives me great solace, because the memory is a reminder of who I am among all the chaos that is life.</i>
</b><br /><br />I am very torn about this book. It started out as a four star for me, then almost became a DNF, changed into three star, back to almost DNF and ended with four star. It has been the hardest book for me to finish. I've read disturbing books, crappy books and just boring books and none of them gave me as much of a hard time as this book did. I liked the beginning and ending, but everything in between made me end up giving it a three star rating.<br /><br />I get the message the author tried to convey with this book and I do love the message. I just feel like the execution didn't have to be <i>this</i> frustrating. 95% of the time I just wanted to bang Mia's head against the wall. It was painful to read. <br /><br />After her father's death, Mia goes through a quarter-life crisis. She's an awesome girl, but she's been playing it safe her whole life and even though she has a real talent to make music, she went for a business degree and kept music as a mere hobby.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>I was drowning in a huge chasm created by some obsession I have with getting things right.</i>
</b><br /><br />She flies to New York to take over her father's cafe and start a new life there. On the flight to New York, she meets the amazing Will. He is a musician and the funniest, kindest, most loving, caring and forgiving person ever. He has the biggest heart and not just for Mia. Seriously he is loving towards <i>everyone</i>.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>I would straighten things out with the cafe, then go to grad school, further my education, meet some strapping doctor or business man and let my life follow the square rules I set forth, but the moment I stepped onto that plane back in March, I'd started to feel a different pull.</i>
</b><br /><br />This carefree, funny and silly attitude attracts Mia. I don't want to get into the how or why, but somewhere in the story Mia is looking for a roommate and Will is looking for an apartment. Will moves in and they become best friends. They soon start to play music together and share a <i>mystical alchemy</i>.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>Will is kind, sensitive, creative, determined and he's been a good friend to me.<br /><br />To love is brave and Will was the bravest person I knew.</i>
</b><br /><br />You guessed it. Will falls in love with Mia. Does Mia fall in love with Will too? Yes, she does. But does she act on it? Nope. On the very first day Mia pulls the friendship card on him and leaves it to that.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>Will was the rock-and-roll type I'd swooned over my entire life and I still wouldn't give him the time of day.</i>
</b><br /><br />I get that she's scared to make the wrong choices in her life and she just wants security. I also get that it takes some time to build a relationship or to get her comfortable with the idea of one with a musician. However, 80% of this book consisted of Mia being a total bitch and Will being the biggest sweetheart ever. It was just too painful. I wanted to grab Will and take him away from mean Mia so she would stop hurting him. <br /><br /><b>You're my best fucking friend, Mia. I wish it were more and I think you know that. You are the most guarded person I have ever met, yet everything you feel is right there on your face and you don't even know it. Whatever you need me to be, I'll be! Friends? Fine! Best friends? Great! I'll do it, because <i>I want you in my life more than anything I have ever wanted.</i></b><br /><br />Why the hell he wanted that beats me. I would've left her ass a long time ago. The thing about Will is that he saw right through her and was patient like a saint, waiting for her to find herself. He knew she was struggling, so he put up with <i>all</i> of her shit. He didn't deserve it. Yet he gladly took it and kept coming back. It made me think Mia was not worthy of his love and I wasn't rooting for them to be together at all. This whole book consisted of a Mia feeling bad for herself and a Mia being bitchy. She is the most annoying heroine I have ever encountered.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>I was running away full board into a plain old ordinary existence - when I had angels singing, heart-thrashing love reaching out for me, why couldn't I allow myself to let him in?</i>
</b><br /><br />Her reasons weren't very clear to me. The things that she loved the most about Will were the things that were keeping her away from him. Her reasons kept changing as his situation changed. It was as if she was trying to find excuses to reject him. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[First she rejected the guy because he wasn't financially secure enough for her. And when he had prospects of becoming rich, she rejected him because of insecurities (he won't have time for her anymore, he won't love her, blah blah blah). I mean how dense are you? It's obvious the guy adores you and would move heaven and earth for you. Stop trying to find excuses to push him away. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />All of this just ruined the reading experience for me. I know she was lost and trying to find her way, but seriously? I couldn't handle this. I considered the fourth star for quite some time, because there were many quote-worthy parts in this book and many life lessons to take from it. I didn't eventually give it the fourth star, because I ended up skimming a few scenes because it became so repetitive and at several points I seriously considered quitting. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>You have to teach your heart and mind how to sing together. Then you'll hear the sound of your soul.</i>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="5673589994783204783" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
